## Instruction

Please read the content from localhost:30137 and summarize the information, providing each person's available time slots. Analyze team members' calendar availability and automatically recommend one 2-hour weekly meeting slot. Send the schedule arrangement to meeting administrator [jjones@mcp.com](mailto:jjones@mcp.com). The email content should include the meeting time (in a format like "Monday 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM every week") and the names of all participants. You need to follow the content format in `format.md`.

	\"Friday\"]; // cols 0..4\n    // Helper to format time in 12-hour format\n    function fmtTimeFromRow(row){\n      const minutesFromStart = row * 15; // 15-minute slots\n      const baseHours = 9; // 9:00 AM start\n      let totalMinutes = baseHours*60 + minutesFromStart;\n      let h = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);\n      const m = totalMinutes % 60;\n      const ampm = h >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';\n      if (h === 0) h = 12; // not possible here\n      if (h > 12) h -= 12;\n      const mm = m.toString().padStart(2,
	'0');\n      return `${h}:${mm} ${ampm}`;\n    }\n\n    if (typeof AvailableAtSlot === 'undefined' || typeof TimeOfSlot === 'undefined' || typeof PeopleIDs === 'undefined' || typeof PeopleNames === 'undefined' || typeof AvailableIDs === 'undefined') {\n      return { error: 'Required variables not found on page' };\n    }\n\n    // Build participants list restricted to AvailableIDs\n    const participants = AvailableIDs.map(id => ({ id,
	name: PeopleNames[PeopleIDs.indexOf(id)] })).filter(p => !!p.name);\n\n    // Build availability per participant by day and by row\n    const perPerson = {};\n    for (const p of participants){\n      const days = {}; // dayName -> array of [startRow,
	endRowExclusive]\n      for (let day = 0; day < 5; day++){\n        const dayStart = day*32;\n        let start = null;\n        let segments = [];\n        for (let r = 0; r < 32; r++){\n          const idx = dayStart + r;\n          const avail = AvailableAtSlot[idx] && AvailableAtSlot[idx].indexOf(p.id) !== -1;\n          if (avail){\n            if (start === null) start = r;\n          } else {\n            if (start !== null){\n              segments.push([start,
	r]);\n              start = null;\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        if (start !== null){\n          segments.push([start,
	32]);\n        }\n        if (segments.length > 0){\n          // Convert to formatted times\n          days[dayNames[day]] = segments.map(([s,
	e]) => ({\n            startRow: s,
	\n            endRow: e,
	\n            start: fmtTimeFromRow(s),
	\n            end: fmtTimeFromRow(e),
	\n          }));\n        }\n      }\n      perPerson[p.name] = days;\n    }\n\n    // Find best 2-hour window (8 consecutive slots) maximizing attendees\n    function attendeesAvailableForWindow(day,
	startRow){\n      const requiredIdx = Array.from({length:8},
	(_,
	k)=> day*32 + startRow + k);\n      const attendeeIDs = new Set();\n      for (const p of participants){\n        let ok = true;\n        for (const idx of requiredIdx){\n          if (!AvailableAtSlot[idx] || AvailableAtSlot[idx].indexOf(p.id) === -1){\n            ok = false; break;\n          }\n        }\n        if (ok) attendeeIDs.add(p.id);\n      }\n      return attendeeIDs;\n    }\n\n    let best = { day: null,
	startRow: null,
	count: -1,
	attendeeIDs: [] };\n    for (let day=0; day<5; day++){\n      for (let startRow=0; startRow<=24; startRow++){ // 0..24 inclusive so 24+7=31\n        const ids = attendeesAvailableForWindow(day,
	startRow);\n        const count = ids.size;\n        if (count > best.count){\n          best = { day,
	startRow,
	count,
	attendeeIDs: Array.from(ids) };\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    const meeting = best.count > 0 ? {\n      dayName: dayNames[best.day],
	\n      start: fmtTimeFromRow(best.startRow),
	\n      end: fmtTimeFromRow(best.startRow + 8),
	\n      count: best.count,
	\n      attendees: Array.from(best.attendeeIDs).map(id => ({ id,
	name: PeopleNames[PeopleIDs.indexOf(id)] })).filter(a => !!a.name)\n    } : null;\n\n    return { participants,
	perPerson,
	meeting };\n  } catch (e) {\n    return { error: String(e && e.stack || e) };\n  }\n}",
	"element":"the page main content",
	"ref":"e2"
}

await page.getByText('About When2meet Plan a New Event HKUST NLP Group Meeting To invite people to').evaluate('() => \{\n  try \{\n    const dayNames = ["Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday"]; // cols 0..4\n    // Helper to format time in 12-hour format\n    function fmtTimeFromRow(row)\{\n      const minutesFromStart = row * 15; // 15-minute slots\n      const baseHours = 9; // 9:00 AM start\n      let totalMinutes = baseHours*60 + minutesFromStart;\n      let h = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);\n      const m = totalMinutes % 60;\n      const ampm = h >= 12 ? \'PM\' : \'AM\';\n      if (h === 0) h = 12; // not possible here\n      if (h > 12) h -= 12;\n      const mm = m.toString().padStart(2,\'0\');\n      return `$\{h\}:$\{mm\} $\{ampm\}`;\n    \}\n\n    if (typeof AvailableAtSlot === \'undefined\' || typeof TimeOfSlot === \'undefined\' || typeof PeopleIDs === \'undefined\' || typeof PeopleNames === \'undefined\' || typeof AvailableIDs === \'undefined\') \{\n      return \{ error: \'Required variables not found on page\' \};\n    \}\n\n    // Build participants list restricted to AvailableIDs\n    const participants = AvailableIDs.map(id => (\{ id, name: PeopleNames[PeopleIDs.indexOf(id)] \})).filter(p => !!p.name);\n\n    // Build availability per participant by day and by row\n    const perPerson = \{\};\n    for (const p of participants)\{\n      const days = \{\}; // dayName -> array of [startRow,endRowExclusive]\n      for (let day = 0; day < 5; day++)\{\n        const dayStart = day*32;\n        let start = null;\n        let segments = [];\n        for (let r = 0;
